FROMWHCD (REAL,12,2,'Frm Warehs Val {F.F}')

TOCUSTCD (REAL,12,2,'To Cust Value {F.F}')
TOWHCD (REAL,12,2,'To Warehs Val {F.F}')

FROMCUSTCD (REAL,12,2,'Frm Cust Value {F.F}')

TOSUPCD (REAL,12,2,'To Vendor Val {F.F}')
TOCUSTCD (REAL,12,2,'To Cust Value {F.F}')
TOWHCD (REAL,12,2,'To Warehs Val {F.F}')
INVCOUNTCD (REAL,12,2,'Inv Count Val {F.F}')
FINCD (REAL,12,2,'Closing Value {F.F}')
USER (INT,13,'User (ID)')
UNIQUE (WARHS,PART,USER)
NONUNIQUE (PART)
NONUNIQUE (USER)
;

STORAGETYPE (INT,13,'Storage Group (ID)')
VELOCITY (CHAR,1,'Velocity')
ALLAISLESFLAG (CHAR,1,'All Aisles?')
UNIQUE (STZONE,STORAGETYPE,VELOCITY)
;

CREATE TABLE ZONESTTYPESAISLES 'Permitted Aisles' 1
STZONE (INT,13,'Storage Zone (ID)')
STORAGETYPE (INT,13,'Storage Group (ID)')
VELOCITY (CHAR,1,'Velocity')
AISLE (CHAR,2,'Aisle')
UNIQUE (STZONE,STORAGETYPE,VELOCITY,AISLE)
;

CREATE TABLE ZOOMCOLUMNS 'Target Zoom Columns' 2
NAME (CHAR,20,'Source Column')
TONAME (CHAR,20,'Target Column')
POS (INT,5,'Pos')
UNIQUE (NAME,TONAME)
;

CREATE TABLE ZPDA_ANSWERS_LOAD 'ZPDA_ANSWERS_LOAD' 0
RECORDTYPE (CHAR,3,'Record Type')
LINE (INT,8,'Ln')
LOADED (CHAR,1,'Loaded?')
KEY1 (CHAR,20,'Key 1')
KEY2 (CHAR,20,'Key 2')
KEY3 (CHAR,20,'Key 3')
CURDATE (DATE,8,'CURDATE')
DOCNO (CHAR,20,'DOCNO')
QUESTF (CHAR,20,'QUESTF')
QUESTNUM (INT,13,'QUESTNUM')
ANSNUM (INT,13,'ANSNUM')
ANSTEXT (CHAR,255,'ANSTEXT')
UNIQUE (LINE)
;
